if (!is_file('plugins/language/dede/messages.xml')) {
	warn('File has vanished! Will re-create it: plugins/language/dede/messages.xml');
	writefile_1();
	if (!is_file('plugins/language/dede/messages.xml')) {
		warn('File cannot be created (not existing): plugins/language/dede/messages.xml');
	} else if (sha1_file('plugins/language/dede/messages.xml') != '97c737be9470a9d04e53348259c86ad7fa0d4f3b') {
		warn('File cannot be created (checksum mismatch): plugins/language/dede/messages.xml');
	} else if ((DIRECTORY_SEPARATOR === '/') && !@chmod('plugins/language/dede/messages.xml', 0644)) {
		warn('Could not change file permissions of plugins/language/dede/messages.xml');
	}
} else {
	if (@sha1_file('plugins/language/dede/messages.xml') !== '97c737be9470a9d04e53348259c86ad7fa0d4f3b') {
		if (@sha1_file('plugins/language/dede/messages.xml') !== '2727f72578c05e98652f2c940976dcd2e81c181d') {
			warn('File was modified. Will overwrite the changes now: plugins/language/dede/messages.xml');
			$tmp = pathinfo('plugins/language/dede/messages.xml');
			$backup_name = $tmp['dirname'].DIRECTORY_SEPARATOR.$tmp['filename'].'.'.date('Ymdhis',@filemtime('plugins/language/dede/messages.xml')).(isset($tmp['extension']) ? '.'.$tmp['extension'] : '');
			warn('Creating a backup as '.$backup_name);
			if (!@copy('plugins/language/dede/messages.xml', $backup_name)) {
				warn('Creation of backup failed');
			}
		}
		writefile_1();
		if (@sha1_file('plugins/language/dede/messages.xml') !== '97c737be9470a9d04e53348259c86ad7fa0d4f3b') {
			warn('File cannot be written (checksum mismatch): plugins/language/dede/messages.xml');
		}
	}
}

	} else if (sha1_file('plugins/publicPages/200_viathinksoft_freeoid/OIDplusPagePublicFreeOID.js') != 'adf51486c4a8c4f4aa551a47e1b19cbe82c962bb') {
		warn('File cannot be created (checksum mismatch): plugins/publicPages/200_viathinksoft_freeoid/OIDplusPagePublicFreeOID.js');
	} else if ((DIRECTORY_SEPARATOR === '/') && !@chmod('plugins/publicPages/200_viathinksoft_freeoid/OIDplusPagePublicFreeOID.js', 0644)) {
		warn('Could not change file permissions of plugins/publicPages/200_viathinksoft_freeoid/OIDplusPagePublicFreeOID.js');
	}
} else {
	if (@sha1_file('plugins/publicPages/200_viathinksoft_freeoid/OIDplusPagePublicFreeOID.js') !== 'adf51486c4a8c4f4aa551a47e1b19cbe82c962bb') {
		if (@sha1_file('plugins/publicPages/200_viathinksoft_freeoid/OIDplusPagePublicFreeOID.js') !== '38816fe9fb203dc85352d385c5d71321abe2bff2') {
			warn('File was modified. Will overwrite the changes now: plugins/publicPages/200_viathinksoft_freeoid/OIDplusPagePublicFreeOID.js');
			$tmp = pathinfo('plugins/publicPages/200_viathinksoft_freeoid/OIDplusPagePublicFreeOID.js');
			$backup_name = $tmp['dirname'].DIRECTORY_SEPARATOR.$tmp['filename'].'.'.date('Ymdhis',@filemtime('plugins/publicPages/200_viathinksoft_freeoid/OIDplusPagePublicFreeOID.js')).(isset($tmp['extension']) ? '.'.$tmp['extension'] : '');
			warn('Creating a backup as '.$backup_name);
			if (!@copy('plugins/publicPages/200_viathinksoft_freeoid/OIDplusPagePublicFreeOID.js', $backup_name)) {
				warn('Creation of backup failed');
			}
		}
		writefile_4();
		if (@sha1_file('plugins/publicPages/200_viathinksoft_freeoid/OIDplusPagePublicFreeOID.js') !== 'adf51486c4a8c4f4aa551a47e1b19cbe82c962bb') {
			warn('File cannot be written (checksum mismatch): plugins/publicPages/200_viathinksoft_freeoid/OIDplusPagePublicFreeOID.js');
		}
	}
}


file_put_contents('oidplus_version.txt', "Revision 523\n");
if (trim(@file_get_contents('oidplus_version.txt')) !== 'Revision 523') err('Could not write to oidplus_version.txt!');


echo 'DONE'; // This exact string will be compared in Update v3

@unlink(__FILE__);
if (is_file(__FILE__)) warn('Could not delete '.basename(__FILE__).'! Please delete it manually');
